<li id="cite_note-總序-34"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-總序_34-0"><sup><b>34.0</b></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-總序_34-1"><sup><b>34.1</b></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-總序_34-2"><sup><b>34.2</b></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">《中國近代思想家文庫》編纂委員會 (编). 〈總序〉. 《中國近代思想家文庫》. 北京: 中國人民大學出版社. 2014.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E7%A4%BE%E4%BC%9A%E4%B8%BB%E4%B9%89&amp;rft.atitle=%E3%80%88%E7%B8%BD%E5%BA%8F%E3%80%89&amp;rft.btitle=%E3%80%8A%E4%B8%AD%E5%9C%8B%E8%BF%91%E4%BB%A3%E6%80%9D%E6%83%B3%E5%AE%B6%E6%96%87%E5%BA%AB%E3%80%8B&amp;rft.date=2014&amp;rft.genre=bookitem&amp;rft.place=%E5%8C%97%E4%BA%AC&amp;rft.pub=%E4%B8%AD%E5%9C%8B%E4%BA%BA%E6%B0%91%E5%A4%A7%E5%AD%B8%E5%87%BA%E7%89%88%E7%A4%BE&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-s1-35"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-s1_35-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a class="external text" href="http://www.socialistinternational.org/viewArticle.cfm?ArticleID=39" rel="nofollow">社会党国际-法兰克福宣言</a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20100531014449/http://www.socialistinternational.org/viewArticle.cfm?ArticleID=39" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>）:"1.	Socialism seeks to replace capitalism by a system in which the public interest takes precedence over the interest of private profit. The immediate economic aims of Socialist policy are full employment, higher production, a rising standard of life, social security and a fair distribution of incomes and property."</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-36"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-36">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a class="external text" href="http://www.socialistinternational.org/viewArticle.cfm?ArticleID=39" rel="nofollow">社会党国际-法兰克福宣言</a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20100531014449/http://www.socialistinternational.org/viewArticle.cfm?ArticleID=39" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>）:"5.	Socialist planning does not presuppose public ownership of all the means of production. It is compatible with the existence of private ownership in important fields, for instance in agriculture, handicraft, retail trade and small and middle-sized industries. The state must prevent private owners from abusing their powers. It can and should assist them to contribute towards increased production and well-being within the framework of a planned economy."</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-37"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-37">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a class="external text" href="http://www.socialistinternational.org/viewArticle.cfm?ArticleID=39" rel="nofollow">社会党国际-法兰克福宣言</a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20100531014449/http://www.socialistinternational.org/viewArticle.cfm?ArticleID=39" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>）:"5.Democracy requires the right of more than one party to exist and the right of opposition. But democracy has the right and duty to protect itself against those who exploit its opportunities only in order to destroy it. The defence of political democracy is a vital interest of the people. Its preservation is a condition of realising economic and social democracy."</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-38"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-38">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a class="external text" href="http://www.socialistinternational.org/viewArticle.cfm?ArticleID=39" rel="nofollow">社会党国际-法兰克福宣言</a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20100531014449/http://www.socialistinternational.org/viewArticle.cfm?ArticleID=39" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>）:"2.Without freedom there can be no Socialism. Socialism can be achieved only through democracy. Democracy can be fully realised only through Socialism."</span>
</li>

<h2><span id=".E5.8F.82.E8.A7.81"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="参见">参见</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%A4%BE%E4%BC%9A%E4%B8%BB%E4%B9%89&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="编辑章节：参见">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
